Accessibility digest

Synopsis

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1179
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1179, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 289. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 16. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 151

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 114 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 39 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 48 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 75

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 73 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 65

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 41 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 23 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 26 (Text has insufficient contrast)
  • Package tenon, test 95, score 7 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 49

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 36 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 16 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 12 (Very low contrast)

Issue titleBad

WCAG: 1.3.1

Score: 38

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test titledEl, score 36 (title attribute belongs to an inappropriate element)

Issue svgImageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 38

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 123, score 36 (svg element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)
